		googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
		googletag.cmd.push(function () {
			googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
			googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
			googletag.pubads().enableLazyLoad({
				fetchMarginPercent: 0,  // Fetch slots within 2 viewports.
				renderMarginPercent: 100,  // Render slots within 2 viewports.
				mobileScaling: 1.0  // same scaling on mobile and desktop.
			});
			googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
			googletag.enableServices();

			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
				var slotId = event.slot.getSlotElementId();
				var slotElement = document.getElementById(slotId);

				if (slotElement) {
					var slotParentElement = slotElement.parentElement;
					if (!slotParentElement) {
						return;
					}
					var isAdParent = slotParentElement.classList.contains('js-ad-slot-parent');
					var isResizeable = slotParentElement.classList.contains('js-resizeable-ad-slot');
					var grayOutSectionOnFailedAdLoad = slotParentElement.classList.contains('js-grayout-ad-slot-on-fail');
					var isFixedHeightForNewAdVariant = slotParentElement.classList.contains('js-resize-fail-add-variant-A');
					if (!isAdParent) {
						return;
					}

					if (isAdParent && !isResizeable && event.isEmpty && !isFixedHeightForNewAdVariant) {
						// Need to handle resizable case
						slotParentElement.style.display = "none";
						return;
					}


					// Update resizeable ad-slot container height
					if (event.isEmpty) {
						if (grayOutSectionOnFailedAdLoad) {
							slotParentElement.style.backgroundColor = '#efefef';
							slotParentElement.style.marginLeft = "16px";
							slotParentElement.style.marginRight = "16px";
							slotParentElement.style.color = "#b5b5b5";
							slotElement.innerText = "AD";
							slotElement.style.alignItems = "center";
							slotElement.style.height = "100%";
							slotElement.style.display = "flex";
							slotElement.style.justifyContent = "center";
						}
						else {
							slotParentElement.style.height = 0;
							slotParentElement.style.margin = 0;
						}
					} else if (!isFixedHeightForNewAdVariant) {
						var adSlotHeight = event.size && event.size[1]; // ad slot size: [320, 50]
						slotParentElement.style.height = adSlotHeight + 'px';
					}
				}
			});
		});
